\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetRange()}{GetRange()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Bio\+Imager.\+Image\+View.\+Get\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

It creates a new \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_imager_1_1_range_tool}{Range\+Tool}} object, which is a form that allows the user to set the range of the data to be displayed.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_imager_1_1_range_tool}{Range\+Tool}} object is created with the following parameters\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item time\+Enabled\+: a boolean that indicates whether the data has a time component.
\item Mode\+: a View\+Mode enum that indicates whether the data is filtered or not.
\item z\+Bar.\+Minimum\+: the minimum value of the z\+Bar.
\item z\+Bar.\+Maximum\+: the maximum value of the z\+Bar.
\item t\+Bar.\+Minimum\+: the minimum value of the t\+Bar.
\item t\+Bar.\+Maximum\+: the maximum value of the t\+Bar.
\item c\+Bar.\+Minimum\+: the minimum value of the c\+Bar.
\item c\+Bar.\+Maximum\+: the maximum value of the c\+Bar.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_imager_1_1_range_tool}{Range\+Tool}} object is then shown to the user.

If the user clicks the

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_imager_1_1_range_tool}{Range\+Tool}} object. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UpdateOverlay()}{UpdateOverlay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Bio\+Imager.\+Image\+View.\+Update\+Overlay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If hardware acceleration is enabled, render the frame. Otherwise, set a flag to update the overlay and invalidate the overlay picture box

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The return value is the value of the last expression evaluated in the method. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
